- **Distance**: ~260 km (6 hrs)
- **Why Visit**: Lush greenery, coffee plantations, Abbey Falls, Dubare Elephant Camp.
- **Weather in May**: Pleasant and misty (~20Â°Câ€“30Â°C).
- **Ideal for**: Nature lovers, couples, and families.

---

### **2. Chikmagalur, Karnataka**
- **Distance**: ~245 km (5.5 hrs)
- **Why Visit**: Coffee estates, Mullayanagiri Peak, Hebbe Falls.
- **Weather in May**: Cool and breezy (~18Â°Câ€“28Â°C).
- **Ideal for**: Trekkers, photographers, and coffee lovers.

---

### **3. Wayanad, Kerala**
- **Distance**: ~280 km (6 hrs)
- **Why Visit**: Waterfalls, caves, tea estates, wildlife sanctuary.
- **Weather in May**: Green and fresh (~22Â°Câ€“32Â°C); pre-monsoon showers possible.
- **Ideal for**: Relaxation and nature trails.

---

### **4. Ooty (Udhagamandalam), Tamil Nadu**
- **Distance**: ~270 km (6.5 hrs)

- **Weather in May**: Very cool and refreshing (~15Â°Câ€“25Â°C).

---

### **5. Kodaikanal, Tamil Nadu**
- **Distance**: ~465 km (9 hrs)

- **Weather in May**: Chill mountain air (~12Â°Câ€“22Â°C).

### **6. Yercaud, Tamil Nadu**
